FAQ / READ ME:
What does this guide cover?
It covers the best possible movesets for every fully evolved/ single evolution Pokemon within the Pokécord bot. These movesets also include moves from pre-evolutions as well. In total, this guide includes Legendary, Mythical and Mega Pokemon. If you’re looking for pre-evolutions, you’re outta luck. If you really want help, shoot me a DM.
Who is insane enough to sink endless hours on something that will eventually be completely outdated?
User o h b o y#2537 on Discord. Yeah I am kind of a maniac, and I definitely have the battle experience to show it. Massive credit to Bulbapedia, where I got all my information as well as other duelling friends who helped me out with this guide.
How do I read this guide? Why are some move names bolded, some moves italicized, and others underlined?
Pokemon are listed in National Dex order, with their typings down below the name. When listing off the moves, I decided the best order to list them are from STAB moves that are always first, and from there decreasing importance in the overall moveset. The following key is needed to understand this importance and order as well:
* BOLD 
   * A moveset must have these moves, no matter what. They are the bread and butter of duelling. 
   * When a Pokemon only has 4 bolded moves and no underlined or italicized moves, it may be possible that some of the moves listed may be filler moves that are almost never useful. However due to a limited level-up moveset, it is best to leave them in there.
   * When a Pokemon has more than 4 bolded moves, it indicates that the last listed bolded moves can be switched out on the fourth slot on a moveset. They all have importance, however with situational context as well.
* UNDERLINED  
   * These moves are only useful in some matchups, but are never more overall important than bold titled moves. 
   * They only are listed when all 4 slots of a moveset are already taken up. Use these according to the situation and at your own discretion.
* ITALICIZED 
   * You should never use these moves, but it may be possible that they may be required in some single matchup (God knows what), perhaps against Pokemon with 4x weaknesses (eg Charizard vs a Rock type move.) 
   * Use with extreme caution. Ignore these moves 99% of the time.
What are these acronyms and odd notes/words you keep using? 
Here is a short summary:
* STAB 
   * Stands for Same Type Attack Boost. If a Pokemon uses a move that has the same type as itself, the move power will gain 1.5 times more damage (EG Charizard using Fly.)
   * You can read more about it here.
* BP
   * Stands for Base Power. Generally is a measure of how powerful a move is, with a higher BP meaning move is more powerful. These are usually 70 BP and above.
* ACC
   * Stands for Accuracy. Each move has a chance of missing out of 100. You want moves that will almost always never miss.  
* For Accuracy
   * Moves with this note are there to cover for more powerful moves that have a decent chance of missing. They usually have lower power, but with a higher accuracy to their counterparts. Guaranteeing a win is key to Pokécord duels, and losing due to chance is awful.
* Both are the same
   * Two moves are exactly the same, and only differ in name and level learned. Only one of these listed is needed.
* Respectively
   * smh
How come some Pokemon forms are listed separately from their base form, while others are not?
When going through the moveset for each Pokemon, I found that the best Pokemon base form movesets differ in some way to their movesets of other forms, be it Mega or Alolan. I also found that these changes in moveset from base form to other forms realistically has little impact. However, I decided to cover the moveset for every Pokemon in this guide. Be sure to check these as you go.
This guide is too long and complicated for use!
If you have trouble finding anything, CTRL + F is your tool. If you find this guide too complicated, just read the bold titled moves and ignore the rest. This should be good enough in the long run. If even that is too complicated, oh well...
For this Pokemon, X move should be listed as more important than Y move. You should change this.
Be aware that the order of moves listed in this guide is purely subjective from my point of view. However for some Pokemon, especially ones with diverse and very useful/ large movesets, I may be wrong with the order. Pokemon like Xerneas, Flygon and Steelix, all with large movesets have left me unsure of what is the optimal moveset for them. Hit me up in the DMs and present your case, and if it is compelling enough, I’ll be happy to change this guide up. However if you plan on doing this, it is extremely likely that you are experienced to the point of not needing this guide.
You made an error! You missed this Pokemon, or this is supposed to say that, or this Pokemon actually learns X move at this level!
I didn’t fully proofread this guide as it is about 400 pages long. If you send me the error in question, I would be happy enough to fix it. If you have any other suggestions about the guide - formatting, etc, I would love to hear feedback.
Will this guide be updated as Pokécord updates roll out?
This guide will be updated on a periodic basis when updates are released. However, what will happen to this guide when TMs are released is indeterminate.
Who can I share this guide with? Do I need to pay anything?
This document is 100% public and free for everyone to use. Feel free to share the link with anybody you want. However I still wish to be credited for the creation of this guide.
Update Log:
2020/05/03
I have been very busy lately with other projects and thus am not up to date with what the latest Galar update entails.  I am planning to finish this latest generation ASAP within my means. If you would like to help me out or receive the latest updates, join the following: 


https://discord.gg/F7yK4Ke

As for my current priorities, they are:
* Fixing movesets of existing Pokemon from SWSH
* Fixing movesets of existing Pokemon in LGPE
2020/05/07
While getting back into Pokecord, I have been learning more about what has changed. As of now, all Pokemon in Sword and Shield from previous games have had their movesets updated to fit these changes. 


As for my current priorities, they are:
* Adding new Galar Pokemon into the guide
* Fixing movesets of existing Pokemon in LGPE
* Fix movesets of Pokemon with previously working moves in Pokecord
2020/05/12
All Galar Pokemon excluding DLC have been added to the guide. My next priority is to fix existing movesets of Pokemon in LGPE as well as Pokemon that got released with Pokemon Home.
2020/05/19
Recent additions include LGPE movesets as well as Pokemon that were added in Pokemon Home. Next priority is fixing movesets with locked moves.
2020/05/21
The guide should be up to date now, aside from various typos and errors! Hooray!
2020/05/30
Pokecord is permanently shut down as announced on the official server. This guide will stay up as a legacy of all my hard work. Thanks to all the users and feedback I have gotten over the years. It was fun listening to you all. Goodbye, for now!
